\subsection{Detailed Description}
Classes specification of the \hyperlink{classtree__node}{tree\+\_\+node} data structures. 

Classes used to described the tree nodes imported from the raw file. The first version of this code is due to Fabrizio Ferrandi, Katia Turati, Giacomo Galbiati

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Fabrizio Ferrandi \href{mailto:fabrizio.ferrandi@polimi.it}{\tt fabrizio.\+ferrandi@polimi.\+it} 

Marco Lattuada \href{mailto:lattuada@elet.polimi.it}{\tt lattuada@elet.\+polimi.\+it} \$\+Revision\$ \$\+Date\$ Last modified by \$\+Author\$ 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{abs\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structunary__expr}{unary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the abs\+\_\+expr node. 

Represents the absolute value of the operand. An A\+B\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR must have either an I\+N\+T\+E\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE or a R\+E\+A\+L\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. The operand of the A\+B\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR must have the same type. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a209a759b9d647795e48cd263093da0c5}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a209a759b9d647795e48cd263093da0c5}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{array\+\_\+range\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structquaternary__expr}{quaternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



struct describing an array range. 

Likewise an array, except that the result is a range (\char`\"{}slice\char`\"{}) of the array. The starting index of the resulting array is taken from operand 1 and the size of the range is taken from the type of the expression. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_adc4cd29d4729ee989edd04a715c1fac8}\label{tree__node_8hpp_adc4cd29d4729ee989edd04a715c1fac8}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{array\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structquaternary__expr}{quaternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Array indexing. 

Operand 0 is the array; operand 1 is a (single) array index. Operand 2, if present, is a copy of T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+UE of the index. Operand 3, if present, is the element size, measured in units of the alignment of the element type. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a58c683e819e54e1c2cec30ac9a817c28}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a58c683e819e54e1c2cec30ac9a817c28}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bit\+\_\+field\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the bit\+\_\+field\+\_\+ref node. 

Reference to a group of bits within an object. Similar to C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+N\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+EF except the position is given explicitly rather than via a F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+D\+E\+CL. Operand 0 is the structure or union expression; operand 1 is a tree giving the number of bits being referenced; operand 2 is a tree giving the position of the first referenced bit. The field can be either a signed or unsigned field; B\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+I\+G\+N\+ED says which. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_ad7edd751db357434c7210b4729b07e47}\label{tree__node_8hpp_ad7edd751db357434c7210b4729b07e47}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{catch\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the catch\+\_\+expr node. 

Evaluate operand 1. If and only if an exception is thrown during the evaluation of operand 1, evaluate operand 2. This differs from T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+I\+N\+A\+L\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR in that operand 2 is not evaluated on a normal or jump exit, only on an exception. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a218a624835787c210f9618eb8ab5996c}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a218a624835787c210f9618eb8ab5996c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{component\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Value is structure or union component. 

Operand 0 is the structure or union (an expression). Operand 1 is the field (a node of type F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+D\+E\+CL). Operand 2, if present, is the value of D\+E\+C\+L\+\_\+\+F\+I\+E\+L\+D\+\_\+\+O\+F\+F\+S\+ET, measured in units of D\+E\+C\+L\+\_\+\+O\+F\+F\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+GN / B\+I\+T\+S\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+IT. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_ae7fdda418794ffed0a1be4ed2428d1ad}\label{tree__node_8hpp_ae7fdda418794ffed0a1be4ed2428d1ad}}

This struct specifies the compound\+\_\+expr node. 

Contains two expressions to compute, one followed by the other. The first value is ignored. The second one\textquotesingle{}s value is used. {\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{cond\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the cond\+\_\+expr node. 

Conditional expression ( ... ? ... \+: ... in C). Operand 0 is the condition. Operand 1 is the then-\/value. Operand 2 is the else-\/value. Operand 0 may be of any type. Operand 1 must have the same type as the entire expression, unless it unconditionally throws an exception, in which case it should have V\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. The same constraints apply to operand 2. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a943666bc1fb1f4e69c7d88477a3b2a33}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a943666bc1fb1f4e69c7d88477a3b2a33}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{convert\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structunary__expr}{unary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This struct specifies the lrotate\+\_\+expr node. 

Shift operation for rotate. Shift means logical shift if done on an unsigned type, arithmetic shift if done on a signed type. The second operand is the number of bits to shift by; it need not be the same type as the first operand and result. {\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{mem\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Memory addressing. 

Operands are a pointer and a tree constant integer byte offset of the pointer type that when dereferenced yields the type of the base object the pointer points into and which is used for T\+B\+AA purposes. The type of the M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+R\+EF is the type the bytes at the memory location are interpreted as. M\+E\+M\+\_\+\+R\+EF $<$p, c$>$ is equivalent to ((typeof(c))p)-\/$>$x... where x... is a chain of component references offsetting p by c. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_acbd950bf489d9dc6e9794126e38083a7}\label{tree__node_8hpp_acbd950bf489d9dc6e9794126e38083a7}}

Used to represent lookup of runtime type dependent data. 

Often this is a reference to a vtable, but it needn\textquotesingle{}t be. Operands are\+: O\+B\+J\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR\+: An expression that evaluates the value to use. O\+B\+J\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT\+: Is the object on whose behalf the lookup is being performed. Through this the optimizers may be able to statically determine the dynamic type of the object. O\+B\+J\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+T\+O\+K\+EN\+: Something front-\/end specific used to resolve the reference to something simpler, usually to the address of a D\+E\+CL. Never touched by the middle-\/end. Good choices would be either an identifier or a vtable index. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_ad0b56816f67568026161e22f9156d817}\label{tree__node_8hpp_ad0b56816f67568026161e22f9156d817}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{placeholder\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structexpr__node}{expr\+\_\+node}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the placeholder\+\_\+expr node. 

Such a \char`\"{}self-\/references\char`\"{} is done using a P\+L\+A\+C\+E\+H\+O\+L\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR. This is a node that will later be replaced with the object being referenced. Its type is that of the object and selects which object to use from a chain of references (see below). No other slots are used in the P\+L\+A\+C\+E\+H\+O\+L\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR. This node denotes a record to later be substituted before evaluating this expression. The type of this expression is used to find the record to replace it. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a5d037f837761da9f01307257e28d4cfb}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a5d037f837761da9f01307257e28d4cfb}}

Reduction operations. 

Operations that take a vector of elements and \char`\"{}reduce\char`\"{} it to a scalar result (e.\+g. summing the elements of the vector, finding the minimum over the vector elements, etc). Operand 0 is a vector; the first element in the vector has the result. Operand 1 is a vector. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_afba0d4a8fc3e215bc0434206ef65943b}\label{tree__node_8hpp_afba0d4a8fc3e215bc0434206ef65943b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{rrotate\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the rrotate\+\_\+expr node. 

Shift operation for rotate. Shift means logical shift if done on an unsigned type, arithmetic shift if done on a signed type. The second operand is the number of bits to shift by; it need not be the same type as the first operand and result. Note that the result is undefined if the second operand is larger than the first operand\textquotesingle{}s type size. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a2426fcdafd15f41efce8eccacf39059e}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a2426fcdafd15f41efce8eccacf39059e}}

The operand may have B\+O\+O\+L\+E\+A\+N\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE or I\+N\+T\+E\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. In either case, the argument will be either zero or one. {\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{try\+\_\+catch\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the try\+\_\+catch\+\_\+expr node. 

Evaluate operand 1. If and only if an exception is thrown during the evaluation of operand 1, evaluate operand 2. This differs from T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+I\+N\+A\+L\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR in that operand 2 is not evaluated on a normal or jump exit, only on an exception. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a5ea5764783c53711244076063a71b3fc}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a5ea5764783c53711244076063a71b3fc}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsave\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structunary__expr}{unary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the unsave\+\_\+expr node. 

The operand is the value to unsave. By unsave, we mean that all \+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+Rs such as T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+Rs, S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+Rs, C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+Rs and R\+T\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+Rs, that are protected from being evaluated more than once should be reset so that a new expand\+\_\+expr call of this expr will cause those to be re-\/evaluated. This is useful when we want to reuse a tree in different places, but where we must re-\/expand. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a928072dcd7c743d2ba2f672987e11b56}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a928072dcd7c743d2ba2f672987e11b56}}

\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{tree__node_8cpp_aa98971385f3d80aebe17503626b829f1}{using\+\_\+decl}}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structdecl__node}{decl\+\_\+node}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



A using declaration. 

U\+S\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+L\+\_\+\+S\+C\+O\+PE contains the specified scope. In a member using decl, unless D\+E\+C\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+E\+N\+D\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+P is true, U\+S\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+LS contains the \+\_\+\+D\+E\+CL or O\+V\+E\+R\+L\+O\+AD so named. This is not an alias, but is later expanded into multiple aliases. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a14c19c038c3e15c33e8b94b2caac9a2f}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a14c19c038c3e15c33e8b94b2caac9a2f}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [128/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{dot\+\_\+prod\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Widening dot-\/product. 

The first two arguments are of type t1. The third argument and the result are of type t2, such that t2 is at least twice the size of t1. D\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+D\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+R(arg1,arg2,arg3) is equivalent to\+: tmp = W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+R(arg1, arg2); arg3 = P\+L\+U\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR (tmp, arg3); or\+: tmp = W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+R(arg1, arg2); arg3 = W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR (tmp, arg3); \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_ac504a376cd26fea102dbac04933b5c46}\label{tree__node_8hpp_ac504a376cd26fea102dbac04933b5c46}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [129/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{vec\+\_\+cond\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Vector conditional expression. 

It is like C\+O\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR, but with vector operands.

A = V\+E\+C\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR ( X $<$ Y, B, C)

means

for (i=0; i$<$N; i++) A\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} = X\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} $<$ Y\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} ? B\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} \+: C\mbox{[}i\mbox{]}; \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a9d2aac92d29e6292b70b2464fd21dff9}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a9d2aac92d29e6292b70b2464fd21dff9}}

\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [130/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{vec\+\_\+perm\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Vector permutation expression. 

A = V\+E\+C\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+R$<$v0, v1, mask$>$ means

N = length(mask) foreach i in N\+: M = mask\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} \% (2$\ast$N) A = M $<$ N ? v0\mbox{[}M\mbox{]} \+: v1\mbox{[}M-\/N\mbox{]}

V0 and V1 are vectors of the same type. M\+A\+SK is an integer-\/typed vector. The number of M\+A\+SK elements must be the same with the number of elements in V0 and V1. The size of the inner type of the M\+A\+SK and of the V0 and V1 must be the same. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a99aeca4b613b3c3a9e5b3d01a55a2bb0}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a99aeca4b613b3c3a9e5b3d01a55a2bb0}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{widen\+\_\+mult\+\_\+hi\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Widening vector multiplication. 

The two operands are vectors with N elements of size S. Multiplying the elements of the two vectors will result in N products of size 2$\ast$S. V\+E\+C\+\_\+\+W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+H\+I\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR computes the N/2 high products. V\+E\+C\+\_\+\+W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR computes the N/2 low products. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a1343f9e5bfd45758e22c6662123484fd}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a1343f9e5bfd45758e22c6662123484fd}}

Unpack (extract and promote/widen) the high/low elements of the input vector into the output vector. 

The input vector has twice as many elements as the output vector, that are half the size of the elements of the output vector. This is used to support type promotion. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_ae6f4e8475d94024bcbfa20eaab2158db}\label{tree__node_8hpp_ae6f4e8475d94024bcbfa20eaab2158db}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{vec\+\_\+pack\+\_\+trunc\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Pack (demote/narrow and merge) the elements of the two input vectors into the output vector using truncation/saturation. 

The elements of the input vectors are twice the size of the elements of the output vector. This is used to support type demotion. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a453c89f644e6b4ed6354373dc56521d6}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a453c89f644e6b4ed6354373dc56521d6}}

Convert floating point values of the two input vectors to integer and pack (narrow and merge) the elements into the output vector. 

The elements of the input vector are twice the size of the elements of the output vector. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a14a4bf5077848dd8d4fb966e9720df20}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a14a4bf5077848dd8d4fb966e9720df20}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [148/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{view\+\_\+convert\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structunary__expr}{unary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the view\+\_\+convert\+\_\+expr node. 

Represents viewing something of one type as being of a second type. This corresponds to an \char`\"{}\+Unchecked Conversion\char`\"{} in Ada and roughly to the idiom $\ast$(type2 $\ast$)\&X in C. The only operand is the value to be viewed as being of another type. It is undefined if the type of the input and of the expression have different sizes.

This code may also be used within the L\+HS of a M\+O\+D\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR, in which case no actual data motion may occur. T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+A\+B\+LE will be set in this case and G\+CC must abort if it could not do the operation without generating insns. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a7454330b0e052f35d5c6b6abd1a03b0b}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a7454330b0e052f35d5c6b6abd1a03b0b}}

\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}

The tree walker structure of this node is\+: \#(T\+O\+K\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE \hyperlink{structtype__node}{type\+\_\+node}); \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a3b724b79dc734df0d87f9bea3a98a37e}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a3b724b79dc734df0d87f9bea3a98a37e}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{vtable\+\_\+ref}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the vtable\+\_\+ref node. 

Vtable indexing. Carries data useful for emitting information for vtable garbage collection. Operand 0\+: an array\+\_\+ref (or equivalent expression) Operand 1\+: the vtable base (must be a \hyperlink{structvar__decl}{var\+\_\+decl}) Operand 2\+: index into vtable (must be an \hyperlink{structinteger__cst}{integer\+\_\+cst}). \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a96bb9c43cb85056f44887a9379d56e84}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a96bb9c43cb85056f44887a9379d56e84}} 
\index{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}!C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}}
\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [151/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{with\+\_\+cleanup\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structternary__expr}{ternary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This struct specifies the with\+\_\+cleanup\+\_\+expr node. 

Specify a value to compute along with its corresponding cleanup. Operand 0 argument is an expression whose value needs a cleanup. Operand 1 is the cleanup expression for the object. Operand 2 is an R\+T\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR which will eventually represent that value. The R\+T\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR is used in this expression, which is how the expression manages to act on the proper value. The cleanup is executed by the first enclosing C\+L\+E\+A\+N\+U\+P\+\_\+\+P\+O\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR, if it exists, otherwise it is the responsibility of the caller to manually call expand\+\_\+start\+\_\+target\+\_\+temps/expand\+\_\+end\+\_\+target\+\_\+temps, as needed. This differs from T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR in that operand 2 is always evaluated when an exception isn\textquotesingle{}t thrown when cleanups are run. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a7d9ecac16829c080cca215d6398b1fce}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a7d9ecac16829c080cca215d6398b1fce}} 
\index{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}!C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}}
\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [152/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{with\+\_\+size\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Records the size for an expression of variable size type. 

This is for use in contexts in which we are accessing the entire object, such as for a function call, or block copy. Operand 0 is the real expression. Operand 1 is the size of the type in the expression. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_aac22c8f242c6afc6807d3d34ff94f9a5}\label{tree__node_8hpp_aac22c8f242c6afc6807d3d34ff94f9a5}} 
\index{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}!C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}}
\index{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS@{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS}!tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp@{tree\+\_\+node.\+hpp}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S()}{CREATE\_TREE\_NODE\_CLASS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [153/155]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{widen\+\_\+sum\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Widening summation. 

The first argument is of type t1. The second argument is of type t2, such that t2 is at least twice the size of t1. The type of the entire expression is also t2. W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+M\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR is equivalent to first widening (promoting) the first argument from type t1 to type t2, and then summing it with the second argument. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_a68264916f73c9cf28874fc54a884635a}\label{tree__node_8hpp_a68264916f73c9cf28874fc54a884635a}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{widen\+\_\+mult\+\_\+expr}]{,  }\item[{\hyperlink{structbinary__expr}{binary\+\_\+expr}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Widening multiplication. 

The two arguments are of type t1. The result is of type t2, such that t2 is at least twice the size of t1. W\+I\+D\+E\+N\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+PR is equivalent to first widening (promoting) the arguments from type t1 to type t2, and then multiplying them. \mbox{\Hypertarget{tree__node_8hpp_adb6370fcb1c07c1813ec41fe30495edb}\label{tree__node_8hpp_adb6370fcb1c07c1813ec41fe30495edb}}
